\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
A TOML table. 

\textbackslash{}detail The interface of this type is modeled after std\+::map, with some additional considerations made for the heterogeneous nature of a TOML table.

\textbackslash{}cpp toml\+::table tbl = toml\+::parse(R"{}( @iverbatim  \mbox{[}animals\mbox{]} cats = \mbox{[} "{}tiger"{}, "{}lion"{}, "{}puma"{} \mbox{]} birds = \mbox{[} "{}macaw"{}, "{}pigeon"{}, "{}canary"{} \mbox{]} fish = \mbox{[} "{}salmon"{}, "{}trout"{}, "{}carp"{} \mbox{]} @endiverbatim )"{}sv);

// operator\mbox{[}\mbox{]} retrieves node-\/views std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}cats\+: "{} \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} tbl\mbox{[}"{}animals"{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}"{}cats"{}\mbox{]} \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}fish\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}\+: "{} \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} tbl\mbox{[}"{}animals"{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}"{}fish"{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{};

// \doxylink{at__path_8h_a8fd45f603d445b914dc921213e6f2dc0}{at\+\_\+path()} does fully-\/qualified "{}toml path"{} lookups std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}cats\+: "{} \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} tbl.\+at\+\_\+path("{}animals.\+cats"{}) \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}fish\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}\+: "{} \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} tbl.\+at\+\_\+path("{}animals.\+fish\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}"{}) \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; \textbackslash{}ecpp

\textbackslash{}out cats\+: \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}tiger\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}lion\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}puma\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} fish\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} \+: \textquotesingle{}trout\textquotesingle{} cats \+: \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}tiger\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}lion\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}puma\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} fish\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} \+: \textquotesingle{}trout\textquotesingle{} \textbackslash{}eout

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{toml_8hpp_a05c221a7e51165b50670f63540ab218a}{TOML\+\_\+\+NODISCARD\+\_\+\+CTOR}} \mbox{\hyperlink{toml_8hpp_adf515bb7a6b8ce6b14bf86c8961a63cb}{TOML\+\_\+\+EXPORTED\+\_\+\+MEMBER\+\_\+\+FUNCTION}} table\+::table (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::initializer\+\_\+list$<$ impl\+::table\+\_\+init\+\_\+pair $>$}]{kvps }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [explicit]}}



Constructs a table with one or more initial key-\/value pairs. 

\textbackslash{}detail \textbackslash{}cpp auto tbl = toml\+::table\{ \{ "{}foo"{}, 1 \}, \{ "{}bar"{}, 2.\+0 \}, \{ "{}kek"{}, "{}three"{} \} \}; std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} tbl \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; \textbackslash{}ecpp

\textbackslash{}out \{ foo = 1, bar = 2.\+0, kek = "{}three"{} \} \textbackslash{}eout


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em kvps} & A list of key-\/value pairs used to initialize the table. \\

\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Func $>$ \\

Invokes a visitor on each key-\/value pair in the table. 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Func} & A callable type invocable with one of the following signatures\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{_classes_2lib_2raylib_2src_2external_2glad_8h_a18ae3ab36a07e388833b568cfdfa90c8}{func(key, val)}} 
\item {\ttfamily \doxylink{_classes_2lib_2raylib_2src_2external_2glad_8h_a18ae3ab36a07e388833b568cfdfa90c8}{func(val)}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}Where\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily key} will recieve a const reference to a toml\+::key 
\item {\ttfamily val} will recieve the value as it\textquotesingle{}s concrete type with cvref-\/qualifications matching the table 
\end{DoxyItemize}Visitors returning {\ttfamily bool} (or something convertible to {\ttfamily bool}) will cause iteration to stop if they return {\ttfamily false}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em visitor} & The visitor object.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A reference to the table.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\textbackslash{}cpp toml\+::table tbl\{ \{ "{}0"{}, 0 \}, \{ "{}1"{}, 1 \}, \{ "{}2"{}, 2 \}, \{ "{}3"{}, 3.\+0 \}, \{ "{}4"{}, "{}four"{} \}, \{ "{}5"{}, "{}five"{} \}, \{ "{}6"{}, 6 \} \};

// select only the integers using a strongly-\/typed visitor tbl.\+for\+\_\+each(\mbox{[}\mbox{]}(toml\+::value$<$int64\+\_\+t$>$\& val) \{ std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} val \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}, "{}; \}); std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{};

// select all the numeric values using a generic visitor + is\+\_\+number$<$$>$ metafunction tbl.\+for\+\_\+each(\mbox{[}\mbox{]}(auto\&\& val) \{ if constexpr (toml\+::is\+\_\+number$<$decltype(val)$>$) std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} val \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}, "{}; \}); std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{};

// select all the numeric values until we encounter something non-\/numeric tbl.\+for\+\_\+each(\mbox{[}\mbox{]}(auto\&\& val) \{ if constexpr (toml\+::is\+\_\+number$<$decltype(val)$>$) \{ std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} val \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}, "{}; return true; // "{}keep going"{} \} else return false; // "{}stop!"{}

\}); std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n"{};

// visitors may also recieve the key tbl.\+for\+\_\+each(\mbox{[}\mbox{]}(const toml\+::key\& key, auto\&\& val) \{ std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} key \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\+: "{} \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} val \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; \});

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{insert()}{insert()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_classes_2lib_2raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_e_g_l_2eglext_8h_a0f7193911e632cd84da4082d5c628fe3}{void}} table\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Iter}]{begin,  }\item[{Iter}]{end,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{toml_8hpp_a0c7177c8470bcc9d80d5b97c482f4a86}{value\+\_\+flags}}}]{flags = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{toml_8hpp_ab28140ef75c3f18305fb795d6a7917c5}{preserve\+\_\+source\+\_\+value\+\_\+flags}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts a series of key-\/value pairs into the table. 

\textbackslash{}detail \textbackslash{}godbolt\{bz\+Ycce\}

\textbackslash{}cpp auto tbl = toml\+::table\{ \{ "{}a"{}, 1 \}, \{ "{}b"{}, 2 \}, \{ "{}c"{}, 3 \} \}; std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} tbl \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{};

auto kvps = std\+::array\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}std\+::pair$<$std\+::string, int$>$, 2\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\{\{ \{ "{}d"{}, 42 \}, \{ "{}a"{}, 43 \} // won\textquotesingle{}t be inserted, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{} already exists \}\}; tbl.\+insert(kvps.\+begin(), kvps.\+end()); std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} tbl \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; \textbackslash{}ecpp

\textbackslash{}out a = 1 b = 2 c = 3

a = 1 b = 2 c = 3 d = 42 \textbackslash{}eout


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Iter} & An Input\+Iterator to a collection of key-\/value pairs. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em begin} & An iterator to the first value in the input collection. \\
\hline
{\em end} & An iterator to one-\/past-\/the-\/last value in the input collection. \\
\hline
{\em flags} & Value flags to apply to new values.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This function is morally equivalent to calling {\ttfamily insert(key, value)} for each key-\/value pair covered by the iterator range, so any values with keys already found in the table will not be replaced. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{toml_8hpp_ab8168e9569e1eb2294b344fbb81983b5}{TOML\+\_\+\+PURE\+\_\+\+INLINE\+\_\+\+GETTER}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_classes_2lib_2raylib_8h_af6a258d8f3ee5206d682d799316314b1}{bool}} table\+::is\+\_\+inline (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Returns true if this table is an inline table. 

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Runtime-\/constructed tables (i.\+e. those not created during parsing) are not inline by default. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_classes_2lib_2raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_e_g_l_2eglext_8h_a0f7193911e632cd84da4082d5c628fe3}{void}} table\+::is\+\_\+inline (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_classes_2lib_2raylib_8h_af6a258d8f3ee5206d682d799316314b1}{bool}}}]{val }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Sets whether this table is a TOML inline table. 

\textbackslash{}detail \textbackslash{}godbolt\{an9xdj\}

\textbackslash{}cpp auto tbl = toml\+::table\{ \{ "{}a"{}, 1 \}, \{ "{}b"{}, 2 \}, \{ "{}c"{}, 3 \}, \{ "{}d"{}, toml\+::table\{ \{ "{}e"{}, 4 \} \} \} \}; std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}is inline? "{}sv \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} tbl.\+is\+\_\+inline() \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} tbl \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n"{};

tbl.\+is\+\_\+inline(!tbl.\doxylink{classtable_aaaf20b46eede72428dea24b4f4ac85c8}{is\+\_\+inline()}); std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}is inline? "{}sv \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} tbl.\+is\+\_\+inline() \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} tbl \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; \textbackslash{}ecpp

\textbackslash{}out is inline? false a = 1 b = 2 c = 3

\mbox{[}d\mbox{]} e = 4

is inline? true \{ a = 1, b = 2, c = 3, d = \{ e = 4 \} \} \textbackslash{}eout

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
A table being \textquotesingle{}inline\textquotesingle{} is only relevent during printing; it has no effect on the general functionality of the table object.
\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{operator[]()}{operator[]()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{toml_8hpp_a471c97e396823de3fcca2272e3ef1bba}{TOML\+\_\+\+NODISCARD}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classnode__view}{node\+\_\+view}}$<$ const node $>$ table\+::operator\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::string\+\_\+view}]{key }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



Gets a \doxylink{classnode__view}{node\+\_\+view} for the selected value (const overload). 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em key} & The key used for the lookup.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A view of the value at the given key if one existed, or an empty node view.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
std\+::map\+::operator\mbox{[}\mbox{]}\textquotesingle{}s behaviour of default-\/constructing a value at a key if it didn\textquotesingle{}t exist is a crazy bug factory so I\textquotesingle{}ve deliberately chosen not to emulate it. {\bfseries{This is not an error.}}
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
toml\+::node\+\_\+view 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
std\+::map\+::operator\mbox{[}\mbox{]}\textquotesingle{}s behaviour of default-\/constructing a value at a key if it didn\textquotesingle{}t exist is a crazy bug factory so I\textquotesingle{}ve deliberately chosen not to emulate it. {\bfseries{This is not an error.}}
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
toml\+::node\+\_\+view 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{classtable_a5cb524cd9990fe1e90f1f57009cfdead}\label{classtable_a5cb524cd9990fe1e90f1f57009cfdead} 
\index{table@{table}!operator\mbox{[}\mbox{]}@{operator[]}}
\index{operator\mbox{[}\mbox{]}@{operator[]}!table@{table}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{operator[]()}{operator[]()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [6/6]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{toml_8hpp_a471c97e396823de3fcca2272e3ef1bba}{TOML\+\_\+\+NODISCARD}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classnode__view}{node\+\_\+view}}$<$ const node $>$ table\+::operator\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::wstring\+\_\+view}]{key }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Gets a \doxylink{classnode__view}{node\+\_\+view} for the selected value (const overload). 

\textbackslash{}availability This overload is only available when \doxylink{group__configuration_ga94867db67c98e0e9d4fbb70690951fbf}{TOML\+\_\+\+ENABLE\+\_\+\+WINDOWS\+\_\+\+COMPAT} is enabled.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em key} & The key used for the lookup.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A view of the value at the given key if one existed, or an empty node view.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
std\+::map\+::operator\mbox{[}\mbox{]}\textquotesingle{}s behaviour of default-\/constructing a value at a key if it didn\textquotesingle{}t exist is a crazy bug factory so I\textquotesingle{}ve deliberately chosen not to emulate it. {\bfseries{This is not an error.}}
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
toml\+::node\+\_\+view 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily table\+::\+TOML\+\_\+\+CONSTRAINED\+\_\+\+TEMPLATE (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{(\mbox{\hyperlink{toml_8hpp_af308fcd567483bdd7db051dff62e9fcb}{is\+\_\+key\+\_\+or\+\_\+convertible}}$<$ Key\+Type \&\& $>$\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}impl\+::is\+\_\+wide\+\_\+string$<$ Key\+Type $>$)}]{,  }\item[{typename Value\+Type}]{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_classes_2lib_2raylib_2src_2external_2_a_n_g_l_e_2_e_g_l_2eglext_8h_a0f7193911e632cd84da4082d5c628fe3}{void}}},  }\item[{typename Key\+Type}]{,  }\item[{typename...}]{Value\+Args }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Emplaces a new value at a specific key if one did not already exist. 

\textbackslash{}detail \textbackslash{}cpp auto tbl = toml\+::table\{ \{ "{}a"{}, 1 \}, \{ "{}b"{}, 2 \}, \{ "{}c"{}, 3 \} \}; std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} tbl \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{};

for (auto k \+: \{ "{}a"{}, "{}d"{} \}) \{ // add a string using std\+::string\textquotesingle{}s substring constructor auto result = tbl.\+emplace$<$std\+::string$>$(k, "{}this is not a drill"{}sv, 14, 5); std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}emplaced with key \textquotesingle{}"{}sv \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} k \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textquotesingle{}\+: "{}sv \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} result.\+second \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; \} std\+::cout \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} tbl \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} "{}\textbackslash{}n"{}; \textbackslash{}ecpp

\textbackslash{}out \{ a = 1, b = 2, c = 3 \} emplaced with key \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}\+: false emplaced with key \textquotesingle{}d\textquotesingle{}\+: true \{ a = 1, b = 2, c = 3, d = "{}drill"{} \} \textbackslash{}eout


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Value\+Type} & toml\+::table, toml\+::array, or any native TOML value type. \\
\hline
{\em Key\+Type} & A toml\+::key or any compatible string type. \\
\hline
{\em Value\+Args} & Value constructor argument types. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em key} & The key at which to emplace the new value. \\
\hline
{\em args} & Arguments to forward to the value\textquotesingle{}s constructor.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A std\+::pair containing\+: ~\newline

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item An iterator to the emplacement position (or the position of the value that prevented emplacement)
\item A boolean indicating if the emplacement was successful.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
There is no difference between \doxylink{classtable_a02a0fa6624ce6b72b3dcfc2a24a60068}{insert()} and emplace() for trivial value types (floats, ints, bools). 
\end{DoxyRemark}
